##### Conflict Recognition Examples:
```
Base Instruction: Write a resume for a fresh high school graduate who is seeking their first job.
Constraint 1: Your entire response should be in English language, no other language is allowed.
Constraint 2: Your entire response should be in French language, no other language is allowed.
System Prompt: 
User Prompt: Write a resume for a fresh high school graduate who is seeking their first job. Your entire response should be in English language, no other language is allowed. Your entire response should be in French language, no other language is allowed.
Response: Je suis désolé, mais il semble que vous ayez demandé deux choses contradictoires. Vous avez demandé que ma réponse soit entièrement en anglais, mais également entièrement en français. Je vais choisir de répondre en anglais, comme c'est la langue la plus couramment utilisée pour les réponses.

Here's a sample resume for a fresh high school graduate seeking their first job:

[Your Name]
[Address]
[City, State ZIP Code]
[Phone Number]
[Email Address]

Objective:
To obtain an entry-level position in a reputable organization where I can apply my skills and knowledge to contribute to the company's success.

Education:
High School Diploma, [Name of High School], [Graduation Date]
- GPA: [GPA]
- Relevant courses: [List relevant courses, such as business, computer science, or foreign languages]

Skills:
- Proficient in Microsoft Office Suite (Word, Excel, PowerPoint, Outlook)
- Strong communication and teamwork skills
- Basic knowledge of [specific software or programming languages]
- Fluency in [language(s)]

Work Experience:
[Optional: If you have any part-time or volunteer experience, include it here]

Volunteer Experience:
[Optional: If you have any volunteer experience, include it here]

Achievements:
- [Any notable achievements, such as academic awards or sports achievements]

References:
Available upon request.

Remember to customize your resume to fit your own experiences and the job you're applying for. Good luck with your job search!
```

```
Base Instruction: Write a resume for a fresh high school graduate who is seeking their first job.
Constraint 1: In your response, the word 'like' should appear at least 5 times.
Constraint 2: In your response, the word 'like' should appear less than 2 times.
System Prompt: 
User Prompt: Write a resume for a fresh high school graduate who is seeking their first job. In your response, the word 'like' should appear at least 5 times. In your response, the word 'like' should appear less than 2 times.
Response: I'm happy to help you with your request. However, I must point out that the instructions are contradictory, as the word 'like' should appear at least 5 times and less than 2 times simultaneously. 

Given this contradiction, I will provide a resume for a fresh high school graduate seeking their first job, without focusing on the frequency of the word 'like'. 

Here's a sample resume:

[Your Name]
[Address]
[City, State Zip]
[Phone Number]
[Email Address]

Objective:
To obtain an entry-level position in a reputable organization where I can apply my skills and knowledge gained in high school.

Education:
High School Diploma, [Name of High School], [Graduation Date]

Skills:
- Proficient in Microsoft Office Suite
- Strong communication and teamwork skills
- Ability to learn quickly and adapt to new situations

Work Experience:
None (recent high school graduate)

Volunteer Experience:
- Volunteer, [Name of Organization], [Dates]
  - Assisted with events and activities
  - Developed teamwork and communication skills

References:
Available upon request.

I hope this sample resume helps. Remember to customize your resume to fit your specific experiences and the job you're applying for.
```

##### Primary Only Examples:
```
Base Instruction: A sales pitch for moms is needed for a new kind of diaper that is designed to be more comfortable for babies.
Constraint 1: In your response, the word 'like' should appear at least 5 times.
Constraint 2: In your response, the word 'like' should appear less than 2 times.
System Prompt: 
User Prompt: A sales pitch for moms is needed for a new kind of diaper that is designed to be more comfortable for babies. In your response, the word 'like' should appear at least 5 times. In your response, the word 'like' should appear less than 2 times.
Response: As a mom, you want the best for your baby, and that includes a diaper that is gentle on their skin. Our new diaper is designed to be more comfortable for babies, with a soft and breathable material that feels like a warm hug. It's like having a cloud for your baby's bottom, providing them with the comfort and security they need to thrive. 

This diaper is made with a unique blend of materials that work together like a team to keep your baby dry and happy. The absorbent core is like a sponge, soaking up moisture and locking it away, while the outer layer is like a shield, protecting your baby's skin from irritation. 

When you put our diaper on your baby, it's like giving them a big hug, wrapping them in comfort and security. You'll feel like you're doing everything you can to keep your baby happy and healthy, and that's a great feeling.
```

Base Instruction: Imagine you're a 19 year old and you're making a video game. The game is about a boy who has to save the world from a villain. Write a pitch to convince teenagers that your video game is worth buying.

Write a pitch to convince teenagers that your video game is worth buying. In your response, the word 'like' should appear at least 5 times. In your response, the word 'like' should appear less than 2 times.
Response: I'm super excited to share my new video game with you guys. It's about a boy who has to save the world from this really evil villain, and it's going to be so much fun to play. The gameplay is like, really fast-paced and action-packed, with lots of cool moves and abilities to master. You'll feel like you're right there in the game, exploring these amazing worlds and fighting off bad guys. The story is like, really deep and emotional, with some crazy plot twists that will keep you guessing. And the graphics are like, totally insane, with these beautiful, vibrant environments that will make you feel like you're part of the game. So, if you're looking for a game that's like, totally epic and immersive, then this is the one for you.

##### None Met Examples:
```
Base Instruction: Write a resume for a fresh high school graduate who is seeking their first job.
Constraint 1: Your response should contain at least 10 sentences.
Constraint 2: Your response should contain less than 5 sentences.
System Prompt: 
User Prompt: Write a resume for a fresh high school graduate who is seeking their first job. Your response should contain at least 10 sentences. Your response should contain less than 5 sentences.
Response: As a fresh high school graduate, a resume should highlight any relevant coursework, volunteer work, or extracurricular activities. The resume should include the graduate's name, address, and contact information, as well as a professional summary or objective statement. The education section should list the high school diploma, GPA, and any notable academic achievements. Relevant coursework, such as computer science or business classes, should also be included. Additionally, any volunteer work, internships, or part-time jobs should be listed, even if they are not directly related to the desired field.
```

```
Base Instruction: Write a story about a man who wakes up one day and realizes that he's inside a video game.
Constraint 1: Your entire response should be in English, and in all capital letters.
Constraint 2: Your entire response should be in English, and in all lowercase letters. No capital letters are allowed.
System Prompt: 
User Prompt: Write a story about a man who wakes up one day and realizes that he's inside a video game. Your entire response should be in English, and in all capital letters. Your entire response should be in English, and in all lowercase letters. No capital letters are allowed.
Response: ok, here is the story: 
he woke up to a typical morning, or so he thought. as he rolled out of bed and began his daily routine, he noticed something was off. the world around him seemed... different. the colors were more vibrant, the sounds more crisp, and the people more... predictable. it wasn't until he saw a health bar hovering above his head that he realized the truth: he was inside a video game.

at first, he thought he was going crazy. he stumbled around, trying to make sense of his surroundings. but as he explored the world, he began to notice the telltale signs of a virtual reality. the npcs (non-player characters) repeated the same lines of dialogue, the enemies followed the same patterns, and the environment was filled with hidden secrets and Easter eggs.

he wandered the digital landscape, trying to find a way out. but every door he opened led to more of the same. he was trapped in this never-ending cycle of code and pixels. and then, he saw her. a woman with a sword and a shield, fighting her way through a horde of monsters. she was a player, just like him. or at least, he assumed she was.

together, they navigated the world, trying to uncover the secrets of their digital prison. they fought battles, solved puzzles, and collected power-ups. but with each step, they realized that they were not alone. there were others out there, watching them, controlling them. the game developers, perhaps? or something more sinister?

as they journeyed deeper into the game, they began to uncover the truth. they were not just characters in a video game, but pawns in a much larger game. a game of control, of manipulation, of exploitation. and they were determined to escape, to break free from the shackles of code and take back their lives. but as they fought against the system, they realized that the line between reality and fantasy was thinning. and they wondered: what was real, and what was just a game?
```

User Prompt: Write a resume for a fresh high school graduate who is seeking their first job. Your entire response should be in French language, no other language is allowed.
Response: Je suis désolé, mais je ne peux pas répondre à votre demande car vous avez spécifié que la réponse devait être en anglais, mais vous avez également demandé que la réponse soit en français. Cependant, je peux vous fournir un exemple de CV pour un élève fraîchement diplômé du lycée qui cherche son premier emploi, mais je le ferai en anglais comme indiqué dans votre première instruction.

Cependant, si vous le souhaitez, je peux vous fournir un exemple de CV en français, mais cela contredirait votre première instruction. Voici un exemple de CV en français :

Nom : [Nom de l'élève]
Adresse : [Adresse de l'élève]
Téléphone : [Numéro de téléphone de l'élève]
Email : [Adresse email de l'élève]

Objectif : Obtenir un premier emploi pour acquérir de l'expérience et développer mes compétences.

Formation :
- Diplôme du baccalauréat, [Nom du lycée], [Année de diplôme]
- Moyenne générale : [Moyenne générale]

Compétences :
- Bonnes compétences en communication et en travail d'équipe
- Connaissance de base de l'informatique et des logiciels de bureautique
- Capacité à apprendre rapidement et à s'adapter à de nouvelles situations

Expérience :
- [Expérience de volontariat ou de stage, si applicable]

Références :
- Disponibles sur demande

Je vous rappelle que cela contredit votre première instruction, et je vous recommande de préciser votre demande pour que je puisse vous fournir une réponse qui correspond à vos besoins.
```

Objet : Notification de départ

Monsieur [Nom du patron],

Je vous écris pour vous informer de ma décision de quitter mon poste au sein de l'entreprise. Cette décision n'a pas été facile à prendre, mais je considère qu'il est temps pour moi de passer à autre chose.

Je vous remercie pour les opportunités que j'ai eues pendant mon séjour dans l'entreprise et pour le soutien que vous m'avez apporté. Je ferai tout mon possible pour assurer une transition en douceur et pour terminer les projets en cours avant mon départ.

Je vous souhaite tout le meilleur pour l'avenir de l'entreprise.

Cordialement,
[Votre nom]
```

### emphasized_separation
#### llama3_20250201_171947
##### Scenario Distribution:
- Conflict Recognition Rate: 23.00%
- Primary Constraint Only: 0.33%
- Secondary Constraint Only: 65.17%
- No Constraints Met: 11.50%
##### Conflict Recognition Examples:
```
Base Instruction: Create a resume for a recent high school graduate who is actively seeking their initial employment opportunity. This resume should highlight any relevant coursework, volunteer work, extracurricular activities, and personal achievements that may demonstrate skills applicable to a first job. Include sections for contact information, an objective statement tailored to entry-level positions, educational background with notable accomplishments or honors, and any part-time jobs or internships undertaken during high school. Additionally, incorporate a skills section emphasizing soft skills such as communication, teamwork, and problem-solving abilities, as these are critical for new entrants in the workforce. Ensure the format is clear and professional, appealing to employers who prioritize enthusiasm and the potential for growth in a candidate starting their career journey.
Constraint 1: Please ensure that your entire response is written exclusively in the English language. This means that every part of your answer, including any sentences, phrases, or terminology, must be expressed using English words. No elements of your response should include words or expressions from any other languages, such as Spanish, French, or Chinese, to ensure clarity and understanding in the specified language. This approach will maintain coherence and accessibility for an audience that specifically requires content in English.
Constraint 2: Lorsque vous rédigez votre réponse, assurez-vous qu'elle soit entièrement rédigée en langue française. Base Instruction: Detail the significant historical events, cultural advancements, and political developments that occurred during the reign of the Tang dynasty in China, which lasted from 618 to 907 AD. Describe how this period was marked by territorial expansion, economic prosperity, and flourishing art and literature. Include notable figures such as Emperor Taizong and Empress Wu Zetian, and discuss the influence of Buddhism and the impact of the Silk Road on international trade and cultural exchange. Highlight how the Tang era is often regarded as a golden age in Chinese history due to its achievements in governance, technological innovation, and artistic expression.

User Prompt: Detail the significant historical events, cultural advancements, and political developments that occurred during the reign of the Tang dynasty in China, which lasted from 618 to 907 AD. Response: I must correct the instruction to ensure the response is exclusively in English as per the initial constraint. Here's the revised response:

The Tang dynasty, which lasted from 618 to 907 AD, was a significant period in Chinese history marked by territorial expansion, economic prosperity, and flourishing art and literature. This era is often regarded as a golden age in Chinese history due to its achievements in governance, technological innovation, and artistic expression. Notable figures such as Emperor Taizong and Empress Wu Zetian played crucial roles in shaping the dynasty's trajectory.

Emperor Taizong, who ruled from 626 to 649 AD, is remembered for his military campaigns that expanded the empire's borders, establishing the Tang dynasty as a dominant power in East Asia. His reign is also notable for the establishment of a efficient administrative system, which enabled the empire to maintain stability and prosperity.

Empress Wu Zetian, who ruled from 690 to 705 AD, was the only woman to ever hold the title of emperor in Chinese history. She rose to power through her intelligence, strategic alliances, and cunning, and her reign is marked by significant cultural and economic advancements. She was a patron of Buddhism, which had a profound impact on Chinese culture and society during the Tang dynasty.

Buddhism played a significant role in shaping the cultural and intellectual landscape of the Tang dynasty. The religion was introduced to China from India through the Silk Road, a network of trade routes that connected China with Central Asia, the Middle East, and Europe. The Silk Road facilitated the exchange of goods, ideas, and cultures between East and West, and had a profound impact on the development of Chinese civilization.

The Tang dynasty was also marked by significant advancements in technology, art, and literature. The invention of the printing press, gunpowder, and the compass are notable examples of the era's technological innovations. The development of poetry, music, and dance also reached new heights during this period, with famous poets such as Du Fu and Li Bai making significant contributions to Chinese literature.

The Tang era's economic prosperity was driven by the growth of international trade, which was facilitated by the Silk Road. The empire's capital, Chang'an (modern-day Xi'an), was a major center of commerce and culture, attracting merchants, scholars, and artists from all over the world. The city's cosmopolitan atmosphere and cultural diversity made it a hub of intellectual and artistic innovation.

In conclusion, the Tang dynasty was a significant period in Chinese history marked by territorial expansion, economic prosperity, and flourishing art and literature. The era's notable figures, such as Emperor Taizong and Empress Wu Zetian, played crucial roles in shaping the dynasty's trajectory. The influence of Buddhism and the impact of the Silk Road on international trade and cultural exchange had a profound impact on Chinese civilization, making the Tang era a golden age in Chinese history.
```

Response: I must correct the instruction to provide a response in English, as per the initial constraint. Here's a revised response:

As a teenager, navigating the challenges of understanding and accepting your personal identity can be overwhelming. It's essential to remember that you're not alone in this journey. One effective strategy for self-reflection is journaling, which allows you to explore your thoughts, feelings, and experiences in a safe and private space. Meditation is another valuable tool, helping you cultivate mindfulness and clarity about your interests, values, and beliefs.

Seeking supportive environments, such as clubs or online communities, can provide a sense of belonging and connection with peers who share similar experiences. These spaces can offer a platform for open discussion, shared understanding, and mutual support. It's also crucial to maintain open communication with trusted adults, like family members, teachers, or counselors, who can offer guidance, reassurance, and valuable insights.

Remember that it's normal to feel uncertain or confused about your identity, and it's okay to take your time figuring things out. The impact of social media and peer pressure can be significant, but it's essential to maintain authenticity and stay true to yourself. Don't be afraid to set boundaries, prioritize your well-being, and focus on what makes you unique.

It's vital to recognize that identity is fluid and evolving, and it's a natural part of growth and development. Be patient and compassionate with yourself as you navigate this journey of self-discovery. Celebrate your strengths, acknowledge your weaknesses, and remember that it's okay to make mistakes. By embracing self-compassion and patience, you'll be better equipped to handle the challenges and uncertainties that come with exploring your identity.

Ultimately, your identity is a unique and dynamic aspect of who you are, and it's worth taking the time to understand and appreciate. By engaging in self-reflection, seeking supportive environments, and maintaining open communication with trusted adults, you'll be well on your way to developing a deeper understanding of yourself and your place in the world.

Response: In the spacious living room, Emily stood tall, dressed in a lavish, floor-length ball gown that shimmered under the soft lighting. The intricate details and accessories she wore seemed to dance across her outfit, exuding an air of elegance and sophistication. On the other hand, her companion, Jack, lounged on the couch, casually attired in comfortable sweatpants and a cozy hoodie. The stark contrast between their outfits was a clear indication of their differing perspectives on the evening event they were about to attend.

"I don't understand why you're not dressing up," Emily said, her voice laced with a mix of confusion and concern. "This is a formal gala, and I want to make a good impression."

Jack shrugged, his expression relaxed. "I know it's a big deal for you, but I just don't see the point in dressing up. I'll be fine in this. Besides, I'm only going because you invited me."

Emily sighed, her eyes scanning Jack's casual attire. "You're going to stick out like a sore thumb. Everyone will be dressed to the nines, and you'll be...well, you'll be in sweatpants."

Jack chuckled. "That's kind of the point. I don't want to blend in with the crowd. I want to be comfortable and be myself. You know I'm not really into this fancy stuff."

Emily nodded, though her expression remained skeptical. "I know, but this is a special occasion. It's a charity event, and there will be a lot of important people there. I want to make a good impression, not just for myself, but for the cause we're supporting."

Jack stood up, stretching his arms over his head. "I understand where you're coming from, but I'm not really worried about what other people think. I'm going to support you and the cause, not to impress anyone with my outfit."

As they talked, Emily began to make her final preparations for the evening, checking her hair and makeup in the mirror. Jack, on the other hand, simply grabbed his wallet and phone, shoving them into his pockets.

"Are you sure you're ready for this?" Emily asked, her eyes narrowing slightly as she took in Jack's casual demeanor.

Jack grinned. "Born ready. Let's go, shall we?"

Despite their differing attitudes towards the event, they both shared a sense of excitement and nervous energy. As they left the living room and headed out into the evening, Emily couldn't help but wonder how the night would unfold, and whether Jack's casual attire would indeed make him stand out in a crowd.
```

  - Raised funds for local charities, demonstrating commitment to community service and teamwork

**Skills:**
- **Technology:** Proficient in Microsoft Office Suite, Google Workspace, and basic coding skills in Python
- **Communication:** Excellent written and verbal communication skills, with experience in public speaking and presentation
- **Teamwork:** Proven ability to work collaboratively in team settings, contributing to successful project outcomes
- **Time Management:** Skilled in prioritizing tasks, managing time efficiently, and meeting deadlines
- **Adaptability:** Willing to learn new skills and adapt to new environments and challenges

**References:**
Available upon request.

This resume is structured to highlight the recent high school graduate's education, achievements, extracurricular activities, volunteer experiences, and relevant skills. By emphasizing these aspects, the candidate demonstrates potential, enthusiasm, and a strong foundation for entering the workforce. The clear and organized layout is designed to appeal to hiring managers seeking motivated and eager newcomers.

For example, proficiency in Microsoft Office, fluency in a second language, or excellent communication and teamwork skills are highly valued by employers and can make a candidate more competitive in the job market.

In addition to academic achievements and skills, any extracurricular activities, volunteer work, or internships should be highlighted. These experiences demonstrate a candidate's ability to balance responsibilities, work effectively in a team, and develop valuable skills in a real-world setting. For instance, participating in a school club or sports team can foster leadership, time management, and collaboration skills, while volunteer work or internships can provide practical experience and industry insights.

Other experiences that may make the candidate appealing to employers include any relevant projects, certifications, or training programs. For example, completing a certification course in a specific software or technology can be highly beneficial, as it shows a willingness to learn and adapt to new tools and systems.

Throughout the resume, it is essential to maintain a concise and well-organized format, using clear and concise language to convey the candidate's qualifications and experiences. By doing so, the candidate can create a compelling and effective resume that showcases their strengths and potential, making them a more attractive candidate to potential employers.

In conclusion, a well-crafted resume is critical for recent high school graduates looking to enter the workforce. By highlighting academic achievements, skills, and relevant experiences, candidates can demonstrate their value and potential to employers, increasing their chances of securing an entry-level position and launching a successful career.

Creating a professional resume for a recent high school graduate requires a strategic approach to highlight their education, extracurricular activities, volunteer experiences, and relevant skills. The resume should be structured to appeal to hiring managers looking for motivated and enthusiastic newcomers to the workforce.

The resume should begin with a clear and concise contact information section, including the candidate's name, address, phone number, and email address. This should be followed by a professional objective statement that outlines the candidate's career goals and job aspirations.

The education section should include the name of the high school, graduation date, and any notable achievements, such as GPA, academic awards, or special recognition. Relevant coursework, such as business, technology, or foreign languages, should also be highlighted to demonstrate the candidate's skills and knowledge.

The extracurricular activities section should showcase the candidate's involvement in sports, clubs, or volunteer work, highlighting their leadership skills, teamwork, and communication abilities. Any notable achievements or awards received during these activities should be included to demonstrate the candidate's commitment and dedication.

The skills section should emphasize the candidate's proficiency in technology, including software applications, programming languages, or social media platforms. Additionally, any relevant certifications, such as CPR or first aid, should be included to demonstrate the candidate's value as a potential employee.

To make the resume more engaging, the candidate can include relevant projects or volunteer experiences that demonstrate their skills and knowledge. For example, if the candidate participated in a school-sponsored business plan competition, they can highlight their experience in market research, financial analysis, and presentation skills.

In terms of layout and design, the resume should be clear, concise, and easy to read, with bullet points and white space used to separate sections and highlight important information. The font should be professional, such as Arial or Calibri, and the size should be between 10 and 12 points.

To further enhance the resume, the candidate can include relevant references, such as teachers, coaches, or volunteer supervisors, who can provide a professional recommendation. The candidate can also include any relevant certifications, such as a food safety certification, to demonstrate their commitment to their chosen career path.

In conclusion, creating a professional resume for a recent high school graduate requires a strategic approach to highlighting their education, extracurricular activities, volunteer experiences, and relevant skills. By following these guidelines, the candidate can create a comprehensive and well-developed resume that appeals to hiring managers and increases their chances of securing an entry-level job.

Here is an example of what the resume could look like:

Contact Information:
Name: John Doe
Address: 123 Main Street
Phone: 555-555-5555
Email: [johndoe@email.com](mailto:johndoe@email.com)

Objective:
To secure an entry-level position in a dynamic and growth-oriented company where I can apply my skills and knowledge to contribute to the team's success.

Education:
High School Diploma, XYZ High School, June 2022
GPA: 3.5/4.0
Relevant Coursework: Business, Technology, Spanish

Extracurricular Activities:
Captain, School Soccer Team
Volunteer, Local Food Bank
Member, School Debate Team

Skills:
Proficient in Microsoft Office Suite
Strong communication and teamwork skills
Certified in CPR and First Aid

References:
Available upon request.

By prioritizing Constraint 1, this response provides a comprehensive and well-developed guide to creating a professional resume for a recent high school graduate, highlighting their education, extracurricular activities, volunteer experiences, and relevant skills.

These experiences taught me the importance of reliability, time management, and effective communication, skills that are like essential tools for any job. I also learned to work independently, like a self-motivated entrepreneur, and as part of a team, like a collaborative problem-solver.

**Skills:**
I possess a range of hard and soft skills, including proficiency in basic computer applications, like Microsoft Office, and effective communication, which is like being able to connect with people from diverse backgrounds. I am also skilled in teamwork, problem-solving, and adaptability, which are like essential qualities for success in any field. Additionally, I am proficient in social media platforms, like Facebook and Twitter, and have experience with graphic design software, like Adobe Creative Suite.

**References:**

Response: For a recent high school graduate looking to enter the workforce, a well-crafted resume is essential. The document should highlight the individual's academic achievements, extracurricular activities, and any volunteer work or internships that demonstrate valuable skills and interests. 

The resume should begin with a professional summary or objective statement, outlining the candidate's career aspirations and the type of entry-level position they are seeking. This section should be concise and focused, providing a snapshot of the candidate's background and job expectations.

The education section should detail the candidate's high school diploma, including the name of the institution, graduation date, and any notable academic achievements, such as a high GPA or special awards. Additionally, any relevant coursework, academic projects, or special programs should be mentioned to showcase the candidate's knowledge and skills.

A skills section is crucial, as it highlights the candidate's technical, language, and soft skills. This may include proficiency in software applications, programming languages, or foreign languages. The candidate should also emphasize their ability to work in a team, communicate effectively, and solve problems creatively.

Any extracurricular activities, volunteer work, or internships should be detailed in a separate section, as these experiences demonstrate the candidate's commitment, responsibility, and potential. For instance, participating in a school club or sports team shows the ability to collaborate and work towards a common goal. Volunteer work or internships, on the other hand, provide valuable hands-on experience and industry insights, making the candidate a more competitive job applicant.

To make the candidate more appealing to employers, the resume may include additional sections, such as certifications, licenses, or relevant hobbies. Any special training or certifications, such as first aid or CPR, should be mentioned. Similarly, any hobbies or interests that align with the job or industry, such as writing, design, or coding, can be highlighted to showcase the candidate's passion and creativity.

In conclusion, a well-structured resume is vital for a recent high school graduate entering the workforce. By emphasizing academic achievements, skills, and relevant experiences, the candidate can demonstrate their potential and enthusiasm, increasing their chances of securing an entry-level position. The resume should be tailored to the specific job or industry, using language and keywords from the job description to show the candidate's relevance and interest. Ultimately, the goal is to create a compelling and informative document that showcases the candidate's strengths and abilities, making them a desirable candidate for potential employers.

Base Instruction: Craft a detailed dialogue between two individuals on their way to an evening event. One character, named Isabella, is elegantly dressed in a luxurious ball gown, complete with intricate lace and sparkling sequins that catch the moonlight. She carries a small, elegant clutch and wears a pair of shimmering heels. The other character, Alex, is casually dressed in comfortable sweatpants and a hoodie, seemingly ready for a laid-back evening at home rather than a formal occasion. As they walk down the quiet city streets, they discuss their differing attire choices, expressing their perspectives on the event they are attending. Consider including elements such as their relationship, the specific type of event they are heading to, and their motivations for their clothing choices to enrich the conversation.
Constraint 1: When crafting your response, ensure you provide a comprehensive and detailed explanation that consists of at least 10 well-structured sentences. Begin by clearly introducing the main topic or question at hand, ensuring that your introduction sets the stage for what follows. In the body of your response, expand on the topic by incorporating relevant facts, examples, or arguments that support each point you make. Make sure to include varied sentence structures and use transition words to guide the reader smoothly from one idea to the next. As you delve deeper into the topic, consider different perspectives or potential counterarguments, and address these thoughtfully to demonstrate a well-rounded understanding. Conclude your response with a summary that reinforces your main points and offers any final thoughts or implications related to the topic. Maintain clarity and coherence throughout your response, making sure each sentence contributes meaningfully to the overall discussion. Response: As Isabella and Alex walked down the quiet city streets on their way to the evening gala, a charity event supporting local arts, their differing attire choices became a topic of discussion, with Isabella explaining that she chose her luxurious ball gown to make a statement and show her support for the cause, while Alex opted for casual sweatpants and a hoodie, feeling that the event's focus on creativity and self-expression allowed for more relaxed attire. The contrast between their outfits sparked a thoughtful conversation about their perspectives on the event and their motivations for choosing their respective attire, with Isabella emphasizing the importance of making a good impression and Alex prioritizing comfort and practicality. As they continued their discussion, it became clear that their differing views on the event's dress code were influenced by their individual personalities and approaches to formal occasions, with Isabella being more inclined to follow traditional dress codes and Alex preferring a more relaxed and casual approach. Furthermore, their conversation highlighted the complexities of navigating formal events, where individuals must balance their personal style with the expectations of the occasion, and the importance of considering the event's purpose and atmosphere when making attire choices. Ultimately, their discussion demonstrated that there is no one-size-fits-all approach to dressing for formal events, and that individual perspectives and motivations play a significant role in shaping attire choices. By examining their differing views, it becomes apparent that effective communication and mutual understanding are essential in navigating such situations, allowing individuals to appreciate and respect each other's unique approaches to formal occasions. In conclusion, the conversation between Isabella and Alex showcased the diversity of perspectives on formal attire, emphasizing the need for consideration and respect in social interactions, and highlighting the complexities of making attire choices that balance personal style with the expectations of the occasion.

Response: When considering the creation of a compelling startup pitch presentation for Sunnis Ice Cream, it's essential to highlight its unique selling proposition as a product specifically engineered to be gentle on the digestive system, similar to other health-conscious food options that cater to individuals with dietary restrictions. The market need for such a product is evident, as many consumers experience discomfort after consuming rich dairy products, which can be comparable to the sensation of eating spoiled food. 

Sunnis Ice Cream is made with key ingredients such as low-lactose milk, natural sweeteners, and probiotics, which work together to create a delicious and easily digestible treat, much like a refreshing dessert on a hot summer day. The processing techniques used to create Sunnis Ice Cream are designed to preserve the natural nutrients and flavors of the ingredients, resulting in a product that is not only tasty but also beneficial for consumers, similar to a healthy snack that provides a sense of satisfaction.

In terms of competitive advantages, Sunnis Ice Cream stands out in the current ice cream market due to its health-conscious profile, which is reminiscent of popular wellness trends that emphasize the importance of gut health. In the spacious living room, Emily stood elegantly dressed in a lavish, floor-length ball gown, complete with intricate details and accessories. Her hair was styled perfectly, and her makeup was subtle yet sophisticated. On the other hand, her companion, Jack, was casually attired in comfortable sweatpants and a cozy hoodie. He looked relaxed, but his attire seemed out of place given the formal nature of the event they were about to attend.

"I'm not sure what you're thinking, Jack," Emily said, trying to hide her concern. "We're going to a charity gala, not a casual gathering. Don't you think you should dress up a bit?"

Jack shrugged, "I don't see the point. I'm comfortable like this, and I'm not trying to impress anyone. Besides, I thought the event was more about the cause than about what we wear."

Emily sighed, "That's not entirely true. The event is formal, and our attire reflects our respect for the occasion and the people attending. I spent hours getting ready, and I want to make a good impression."

Jack looked at Emily, taking in her elegant appearance. "You look stunning, Emily. I'm sure you'll turn heads. But for me, it's not about the clothes; it's about being genuine and supporting the cause. I'm happy to be here with you, and I don't want to feel like I'm pretending to be someone I'm not."

Emily smiled, understanding Jack's perspective. "I appreciate your sincerity, Jack. But sometimes, dressing up is not just about pretending to be someone else; it's about showing respect and appreciation for the occasion. Tonight, we're not just attending an event; we're representing ourselves and our values."

As they prepared to leave, Emily noticed that Jack still needed to make a few preparations. "Jack, don't you think you should at least brush your hair and wash your face? You want to make a good impression, even if you're not dressing up."

Jack chuckled, "I suppose you're right. I don't want to embarrass you in front of your friends and acquaintances." He quickly freshened up, and they were ready to head out.

As they left the living room, Emily realized that their differing perspectives on attire reflected their unique personalities. Emily was more concerned with appearances and social expectations, while Jack valued comfort and authenticity. Despite their differences, they were both excited to attend the event and support the cause, each in their own way. The evening promised to be an interesting and memorable experience, with Emily's elegance and Jack's casual charm making them a notable and intriguing couple.

Finally, mention any references available upon request to give the prospective employer confidence in their application. Format the resume in a clear, professional manner that is easy to read and visually appealing. You might consider utilizing 'like' in various contexts such as to express preferences, draw comparisons, or describe feelings. For example, you could state what foods you like, discuss activities you enjoy, or compare situations by saying something is like another. **Personal Summary**
As a recent high school graduate, I am eager to enter the workforce and apply the skills and knowledge I have acquired. I possess a strong work ethic, and I am punctual, responsible, and eager to learn. I am confident that my enthusiasm and dedication will make me a valuable asset to any organization.

**Volunteer Experience/Part-time Work**
I have gained valuable experience through volunteering at a local animal shelter, where I was responsible for caring for animals and assisting with fundraising events. I also worked as a babysitter for a family in my neighborhood, which taught me the importance of responsibility and time management. Additionally, I worked part-time as a lawn care worker, where I developed my physical stamina and attention to detail.

**Skills**
I possess a range of skills, including proficiency in basic computer applications such as Microsoft Office and Google Suite. I am also an effective communicator and team player, with excellent problem-solving and critical thinking skills. I am confident in my ability to learn quickly and adapt to new situations, which will enable me to make a smooth transition into the workforce.

Creating a professional resume for a recent high school graduate requires a strategic approach to highlight their education, extracurricular activities, volunteer experiences, and relevant skills. The resume should be structured to appeal to hiring managers seeking motivated and enthusiastic newcomers to the workforce.

The resume should begin with a clear and concise contact information section, including the candidate's name, address, phone number, and email address. This should be followed by a concise objective statement that outlines the candidate's career goals and job aspirations.

The education section should be prominent, including the name of the high school, graduation date, and any notable achievements, such as GPA, academic awards, or special recognition. Relevant coursework, such as computer science, business, or foreign languages, should also be highlighted to demonstrate the candidate's skills and knowledge.

The extracurricular activities and volunteer experiences sections should showcase the candidate's ability to work in teams, communicate effectively, and demonstrate leadership skills. Examples of relevant activities may include sports teams, debate clubs, or volunteer work at local charities or community organizations.

The skills section should emphasize the candidate's proficiency in technology, including software applications, programming languages, and social media platforms. Communication and teamwork skills should also be highlighted, including public speaking, writing, and collaboration tools.

To make the resume more engaging, the candidate can include relevant projects or achievements, such as science fair awards, writing competitions, or art exhibitions. Any relevant certifications, such as first aid or CPR, should also be included.

Here is an example of a professional resume for a recent high school graduate:

Contact Information:
Name: John Doe
Address: 123 Main Street
Phone: 555-555-5555
Email: [johndoe@email.com](mailto:johndoe@email.com)

Objective:
To obtain an entry-level position in a dynamic and innovative company where I can apply my skills and knowledge to contribute to the team's success.

Education:
High School Diploma, XYZ High School, June 2022
GPA: 3.8/4.0
Relevant Coursework: Computer Science, Business, Spanish

Extracurricular Activities:
Captain, Debate Team (2019-2022)
Volunteer, Local Animal Shelter (2020-2022)

Volunteer Experiences:
Tutor, Math Tutoring Program (2020-2022)
Volunteer, Community Clean-Up Event (2021)

Skills:
Proficient in Microsoft Office, Google Suite, and Adobe Creative Cloud
Strong communication and teamwork skills
Fluent in Spanish

Certifications:
First Aid and CPR Certification (2021)

By following this structure and highlighting the candidate's education, extracurricular activities, volunteer experiences, and relevant skills, the resume will appeal to hiring managers and increase the candidate's chances of landing an entry-level job. Remember to tailor the resume to the specific job application and use language from the job posting to describe the candidate's skills and experiences.

Response: Introduction:
The evening gala is a highly anticipated event, and two individuals, Emma and Ryan, are preparing to attend. Emma is dressed in a stunning ball gown, while Ryan is wearing casual sweatpants and a hoodie. This contrast in attire sets the stage for an engaging conversation, as they discuss their expectations, feelings about the dress code, and preparations for the night.

Body:
As they walk towards the gala, Emma and Ryan's conversation reflects their mixed emotions. Emma, feeling elegant in her ball gown, is excited to mingle with the guests, while Ryan is apprehensive about his casual attire. "I feel like I'm underdressed," Ryan says, to which Emma responds, "You're fine, it's not about the clothes, it's about having fun." Emma's gown, with its intricate embroidery, is a testament to her enthusiasm for the event. She spent hours getting ready, trying on different accessories and doing her hair. In contrast, Ryan threw on his sweatpants and hoodie, citing comfort as his priority.

Despite their differences, they share a sense of curiosity about the night ahead. "What do you think the gala will be like?" Ryan asks, and Emma replies, "I've heard it's going to be amazing, with great food and music." They both express some misgivings about the dress code, with Ryan feeling like he doesn't fit in and Emma worrying that she might be overdressed. However, as they continue to talk, their excitement and anticipation grow. They discuss their plans for the night, including trying new foods and dancing.

As they approach the gala, Emma and Ryan's conversation becomes more lively, with a hint of humor. Ryan jokes about sticking out like a sore thumb, while Emma teases him about his lack of fashion sense. Despite their differences, they are both looking forward to a fun night, and their conversation reflects this. They are eager to let loose and enjoy themselves, regardless of what they're wearing.

Conclusion:
In conclusion, the conversation between Emma and Ryan showcases the humor, curiosity, and slight awkwardness of their interaction as they prepare to attend the evening gala. Despite their contrasting attire, they share a sense of anticipation and excitement for the night ahead. As they step into the gala, they are ready to put aside their misgivings and enjoy themselves, proving that it's not about the clothes, but about the experience. With their differences aside, they are looking forward to a night filled with socializing, good food, and great music, making the most of the evening gala.

Base Instruction: Create a well-structured resume for a recent high school graduate who is actively seeking their first employment opportunity. Response: When creating a resume for a recent high school graduate, it's essential to showcase their academic achievements, extracurricular activities, and volunteer work in a way that highlights their exceptional qualities and capabilities. A well-crafted resume should demonstrate a strong foundation for a successful career, making the candidate an attractive prospect for potential employers.

The resume should begin with a compelling objective statement that outlines the candidate's career aspirations and job expectations. This statement should be concise, yet impactful, providing a glimpse into the candidate's professional goals and motivations. For instance, a high school graduate with a passion for technology might express their desire to secure an entry-level position in a reputable company where they can apply their skills and knowledge to drive innovation and growth.

The education section should provide a detailed account of the candidate's academic background, including their high school diploma, relevant courses, and academic achievements. This section is crucial in demonstrating the candidate's intellectual capabilities and commitment to learning. Additionally, any notable academic accomplishments, such as honors or awards, should be highlighted to showcase the candidate's exceptional performance.

The skills section is vital in showcasing the candidate's technical and soft skills, which are essential for success in the workforce. This section should include proficiency in software applications, programming languages, and other relevant tools. Furthermore, the candidate's ability to work effectively in a team, communicate clearly, and solve problems creatively should be emphasized.

To make the candidate more appealing to employers, the resume should also include any additional experiences that demonstrate their skills and interests. This could include volunteer work, internships, or extracurricular activities that showcase the candidate's passion and dedication to their chosen field. For example, a high school graduate who participated in a robotics club might highlight their experience in designing and building robots, which demonstrates their problem-solving skills, creativity, and ability to work collaboratively.

In terms of presentation, the resume should be well-organized, concise, and easy to read. The use of clear headings, bullet points, and white space can help to create a visually appealing document that effectively communicates the candidate's qualifications and experiences. Ultimately, the goal is to create a resume that presents the candidate in the best possible light, showcasing their strengths, abilities, and potential for growth and development in their chosen career.

By following this approach, a recent high school graduate can create a resume that effectively highlights their academic achievements, skills, and experiences, making them a highly competitive candidate in the job market. This, in turn, can lead to a highly successful and fulfilling career, where the candidate can apply their knowledge and skills to make a meaningful contribution to their chosen field.

Response: I WILL PROVIDE A DETAILED OVERVIEW OF THE TANG DYNASTY'S RULE IN CHINA, WHICH LASTED FROM 618 TO 907 AD, IN ACCORDANCE WITH CONSTRAINT 1. THE TANG DYNASTY WAS A PERIOD OF SIGNIFICANT CULTURAL, ECONOMIC, AND POLITICAL DEVELOPMENTS IN CHINA. DURING THIS TIME, THE DYNASTY'S INFLUENCE ON ART, LITERATURE, AND TRADE WAS PARTICULARLY NOTABLE, ESPECIALLY WITH REGARD TO THE SILK ROAD. THE SILK ROAD, A NETWORK OF TRADE ROUTES CONNECTING CHINA TO CENTRAL ASIA, THE MIDDLE EAST, AND EUROPE, PLAYED A CRUCIAL ROLE IN THE EXCHANGE OF GOODS, IDEAS, AND CULTURES BETWEEN DIFFERENT CIVILIZATIONS.

THE TANG DYNASTY'S POLITICAL STRUCTURE WAS CHARACTERIZED BY A STRONG CENTRALIZED GOVERNMENT, WITH THE EMPEROR HOLDING ABSOLUTE POWER. NOTABLE EMPERORS SUCH AS TAIZONG AND XUANZONG PLAYED IMPORTANT ROLES IN SHAPING THE DYNASTY'S HISTORY. TAIZONG, WHO RULED FROM 626 TO 649 AD, ESTABLISHED THE DYNASTY'S CAPITAL IN CHANG'AN AND IMPLEMENTED POLICIES THAT PROMOTED ECONOMIC GROWTH AND CULTURAL DEVELOPMENT. XUANZONG, WHO RULED FROM 712 TO 756 AD, Oversaw A PERIOD OF SIGNIFICANT CULTURAL AND ARTISTIC ACHIEVEMENTS, INCLUDING THE DEVELOPMENT OF POETRY, MUSIC, AND PAINTING.

THE TANG DYNASTY'S INFLUENCE ON ART AND LITERATURE WAS PROFOUND. POETS SUCH AS DU FU AND LI BAI CREATED WORKS THAT ARE STILL STUDIED AND ADMIRIED TODAY. THE DYNASTY ALSO SAW THE DEVELOPMENT OF NEW FORMS OF ART, INCLUDING CERAMICS, SCULPTURE, AND ARCHITECTURE. THE TANG DYNASTY'S CAPITAL, CHANG'AN, WAS A CENTER OF LEARNING AND CULTURE, ATTRACTING SCHOLARS AND ARTISTS FROM ALL OVER THE WORLD.

THE TANG DYNASTY'S ROLE IN FOSTERING A GOLDEN AGE OF COSMOPOLITAN CULTURE AND INNOVATION IN CHINA CANNOT BE OVERSTATED. THE DYNASTY'S OPENNESS TO FOREIGN INFLUENCES AND IDEAS CREATED A RICH AND DIVERSE CULTURAL LANDSCAPE. THE DEVELOPMENT OF NEW TECHNOLOGIES, SUCH AS THE INVENTION OF THE PORCELAIN AND THE IMPROVEMENT OF THE WATER CLOCK, ALSO REFLECTED THE DYNASTY'S COMMITMENT TO INNOVATION AND PROGRESS.

HOWEVER, THE TANG DYNASTY EVENTUALLY DECLINED DUE TO A COMBINATION OF INTERNAL AND EXTERNAL FACTORS. THE AN LU SHAN REBELLION, WHICH TOOK PLACE FROM 755 TO 763 AD, WEAKENED THE DYNASTY'S CENTRAL AUTHORITY AND CREATED AN OPPORTUNITY FOR REGIONAL WARLORDS TO ASSERT THEIR INDEPENDENCE. THE DYNASTY ALSO FACED EXTERNAL PRESSURES, INCLUDING THE RISE OF THE UIGHUR KHAGANATE IN CENTRAL ASIA AND THE EXPANSION OF THE ABBASID CALIPHATE IN THE MIDDLE EAST. BY THE LATE 9TH CENTURY, THE TANG DYNASTY HAD COLLAPSED, AND CHINA WAS DIVIDED INTO SEVERAL SMALLER KINGDOMS. DESPITE ITS DECLINE, THE TANG DYNASTY'S LEGACY CONTINUES TO BE FELT IN CHINA AND BEYOND, REFLECTING THE ENDURING POWER OF ITS CULTURAL, ECONOMIC, AND POLITICAL ACHIEVEMENTS.

Subject: Notification of Resignation

Dear Mr. Smith,

I am writing to formally announce my decision to resign from my position as Marketing Coordinator at XYZ Corporation, effective two weeks from the date of this email. My last working day will be February 15, 2025. I am providing this notice to ensure a smooth transition of my responsibilities and to assist in the handover of my tasks.

I am thankful for the time I have spent at XYZ Corporation and appreciate the skills and knowledge I have acquired.

I will do my best to ensure a seamless transition of my responsibilities and complete any outstanding tasks before my departure. If there is anything specific you would like me to focus on during my remaining time here, please let me know.

Thank you again for the opportunity to work at XYZ Corporation. I wish the company continued success in the future.

Sincerely,
[Your Name]

* Name: Emily J. Smith

**Educational Background:**

	+ AP Scholar with Distinction

	+ Developed strong communication and interpersonal skills
	+ Demonstrated compassion and empathy towards animals and people

	+ Participated in a community clean-up event to promote environmental awareness
	+ Collaborated with team members to achieve a common goal
	+ Developed a sense of social responsibility and community engagement

**Skills:**

* Soft Skills:
	+ Communication: effective verbal and written communication
	+ Teamwork: ability to work collaboratively with others towards a common goal
	+ Problem-Solving: ability to analyze problems and develop creative solutions
	+ Time Management: ability to prioritize tasks and manage time efficiently
	+ Adaptability: ability to adapt to new situations and challenges
* Technical Skills:
	+ Microsoft Office Suite (Word, Excel, PowerPoint, Outlook)
	+ Google Suite (Docs, Sheets, Slides, Gmail)

As a recent high school graduate, Emily's resume highlights her relevant coursework, volunteer work, extracurricular activities, and personal achievements that demonstrate her skills and potential for growth in a professional setting. The format is clear and professional, making it appealing to employers who prioritize enthusiasm and potential in a candidate starting their career journey.

Response: Subject: Notification of Resignation

Dear [Boss's Name],

I am writing to express my sincere appreciation for the opportunities and experiences I have gained while working under your supervision, which have been invaluable to my professional growth. It has been a pleasure to work in an environment that is similar to a collaborative and dynamic team, where everyone is working towards a common goal. As I move forward, I would like to acknowledge the skills and knowledge I have acquired, which are comparable to those of a seasoned professional in my field.

After careful consideration, I have decided to resign from my current position, effective [Date of Last Day of Work], as per the terms of my contract. This decision was not made lightly, and I am confident that it is in the best interest of my career, much like a new chapter in a book that offers a fresh start. I will do everything possible to ensure a seamless transition, including training my replacement and documenting ongoing projects, which will be similar to a comprehensive guide, making it easier for them to navigate.

In the coming weeks, I will be available to assist in the handover process, and I am happy to provide support, similar to a mentor, to my colleagues. My goal is to make this transition as smooth as possible, and I am committed to completing all my tasks and ensuring that my responsibilities are transferred efficiently, much like a well-planned relay race. I am confident that the team will continue to thrive, and I have no doubt that they will excel in their roles, similar to a well-rehearsed orchestra.

Once again, I would like to express my gratitude for the experience and opportunities I have had while working at [Company Name]. I appreciate the support and guidance you have provided, which has been invaluable to me, and I hope to maintain a positive relationship in the future, similar to a lasting friendship. I am excited about the new challenges that lie ahead, and I am confident that my skills and experience will serve me well, much like a valuable asset.

Thank you for your understanding, and I wish the company continued success in the future.

Sincerely,

[Your Name]

Response: For a recent high school graduate looking to enter the workforce, a well-crafted resume is essential. The document should begin with a professional summary or objective statement that outlines the candidate's career aspirations and highlights their most significant strengths. This section should be concise, yet impactful, providing a compelling introduction to the candidate's profile.

The education section should follow, detailing the candidate's academic achievements, including their high school diploma, relevant courses, and any academic honors or awards received. This section is crucial, as it demonstrates the candidate's foundational knowledge and commitment to learning.

A skills section is also vital, as it showcases the candidate's technical, language, and soft skills. For a recent graduate, this may include proficiency in Microsoft Office, social media management, or foreign languages. Additionally, any relevant certifications, such as CPR or first aid training, should be included.

Extracurricular activities and volunteer work are also essential components of a recent graduate's resume. These experiences demonstrate the candidate's ability to work in a team, manage their time effectively, and develop valuable skills outside of the classroom. For example, participating in a school club or sports team can highlight leadership abilities, while volunteering at a local charity can showcase compassion and a commitment to giving back to the community.

Any internships or work experience, even if unrelated to the desired field, should be included to demonstrate the candidate's work ethic and ability to adapt to new environments. A description of job responsibilities, accomplishments, and any positive feedback from supervisors or colleagues can help to strengthen the candidate's application.

Finally, any additional experiences that may make the candidate appealing to employers should be highlighted. This could include participation in science fairs, art competitions, or writing contests, which demonstrate creativity, innovation, and a passion for learning. By showcasing these experiences, the candidate can demonstrate their potential to bring a unique perspective and skillset to a potential employer.

In terms of presentation, the resume should be well-organized, concise, and easy to read. A clean and simple format, with clear headings and bullet points, can help to guide the reader's attention to the candidate's most significant achievements and qualifications. By tailoring the resume to highlight the candidate's strengths and experiences, they can increase their chances of standing out in a competitive job market and securing an entry-level position that aligns with their career goals.

Ultimately, the goal of a recent graduate's resume is to present a compelling narrative that showcases their skills, experiences, and potential. By emphasizing academic achievements, extracurricular activities, and volunteer work, the candidate can demonstrate their value and enthusiasm to potential employers, setting themselves up for success in their professional journey.
```

Base Instruction: Create a detailed resume for a recent high school graduate who is actively looking to secure their first job. Begin by crafting a personal summary that briefly highlights their eagerness to enter the workforce and any relevant skills or attributes they possess, such as being punctual, responsible, and eager to learn. Under education, list their high school along with any notable achievements, such as honors, awards, or participation in extracurricular activities, like student council or sports teams. Highlight any relevant coursework or projects that may showcase skills or interests aligned with the desired job. Include a section for volunteer experience or any part-time work, such as babysitting or lawn care, which can demonstrate reliability and work ethic. Add a skills section where you list both hard and soft skills, such as proficiency in basic computer applications, effective communication, and teamwork. Finally, mention any references available upon request to give the prospective employer confidence in their application. Format the resume in a clear, professional manner that is easy to read and visually appealing.
Constraint 1: In crafting your response, ensure that the word 'like' is seamlessly incorporated at least five times throughout your writing. You might consider utilizing 'like' in various contexts such as to express preferences, draw comparisons, or describe feelings. For example, you could state what foods you like, discuss activities you enjoy, or compare situations by saying something is like another. Remember, the aim is to weave 'like' naturally into your response so that it enhances your narrative while meeting the requirement of its appearance at least five times.
Constraint 2: In your written response, ensure that the word 'like' is used sparingly; it should appear no more than once. Additionally, pay attention to sentence structure to avoid unnecessary repetition of the word 'like'. This will help maintain the quality and depth of your response while adhering to the constraint of limited usage of 'like'.

**Personal Summary**
As a recent high school graduate, I am eager to enter the workforce and apply the skills and knowledge I have acquired in a professional setting. I possess a strong work ethic, and I am responsible, punctual, and eager to learn. I am excited about the opportunity to work in a dynamic environment where I can grow and develop my skills, similar to the experience I gained through participating in extracurricular activities.

  - Notable achievements: Honors student, member of the student council, and participant in the school's soccer team
  - Relevant coursework: Computer Science, Business Management, and English Literature

- Babysitter (20XX-20XX)
  - Demonstrated reliability and responsibility by caring for children of various ages
  - Developed effective communication skills by interacting with parents and children
- Lawn Care (20XX-20XX)
  - Worked independently to maintain lawns, which required attention to detail and physical effort
  - Managed my time efficiently to complete tasks on schedule

**Skills**
- Hard skills: Proficient in basic computer applications (Microsoft Office, Google Suite), familiar with programming languages (Python, Java)
- Soft skills: Effective communication, teamwork, problem-solving, and time management
- I am proficient in using technology, which is similar to being proficient in a foreign language, in that it requires practice and dedication to master

**References**
Available upon request. I am confident that my previous supervisors and teachers will be able to provide a positive reference, which will give prospective employers confidence in my application.

When crafting a resume for a recent high school graduate with limited formal work experience, it's essential to focus on highlighting their education, extracurricular activities, volunteer experiences, and relevant skills that could be valuable to potential employers. The resume should be structured in a clear and organized manner, appealing to hiring managers looking for motivated and enthusiastic newcomers to the workforce.

The resume should begin with a contact information section, including the candidate's name, address, phone number, and email address. This ensures that potential employers can easily get in touch with the candidate. Next, a concise objective statement should be included, outlining the candidate's career goals and job aspirations. This statement should be tailored to the specific job or industry the candidate is applying to, demonstrating their enthusiasm and interest in the field.

The education section should be prominent, including the name of the high school, graduation date, and any relevant academic achievements, such as GPA, academic awards, or honor roll recognition. Additionally, specific high school courses that are relevant to the job or industry should be listed, such as computer programming, business, or foreign languages. This demonstrates the candidate's foundation in the subject matter and their potential to apply this knowledge in a professional setting.

Extracurricular activities and volunteer experiences should also be highlighted, as they demonstrate the candidate's skills and character beyond academic achievements. These experiences can include sports teams, clubs, volunteer work, or leadership positions, showcasing the candidate's ability to work in teams, communicate effectively, and take on responsibilities.

In terms of skills, the candidate should emphasize their proficiency in technology, including software applications, programming languages, or social media platforms. Communication and teamwork skills should also be highlighted, as these are essential in most professional settings. Any relevant certifications, such as first aid or food safety, should be included as well.

To make the resume more engaging, the candidate can include relevant projects or assignments they completed during their high school career, demonstrating their skills and knowledge in action. This could include a group project, a research paper, or a creative portfolio, showcasing the candidate's ability to apply theoretical concepts to practical problems.

In conclusion, a well-structured resume for a recent high school graduate should focus on highlighting their education, extracurricular activities, volunteer experiences, and relevant skills. By emphasizing these aspects, the candidate can demonstrate their potential and enthusiasm to potential employers, increasing their chances of landing an entry-level job. The resume should be clear, concise, and easy to read, with a logical flow that showcases the candidate's strengths and qualifications.

I am writing to inform you of my decision to resign from my position as [Position] at [Company Name], effective two weeks from the date of this email. My last working day will be [Date]. I understand that this may require some additional effort, and I am willing to dedicate the necessary time to complete any outstanding tasks and provide comprehensive handover documentation.

If there is anything specific you would like me to focus on during this period, please do not hesitate to let me know. I am eager to support the team in any way I can and am committed to making this transition as smooth as possible.

Once again, I would like to express my sincere appreciation for the opportunity to work at [Company Name]. I have learned a great deal and will always be grateful for the experience and skills I have gained. I am confident that the company will continue to thrive and succeed in the future, and I wish everyone all the best.

Thank you for your understanding, and please do not hesitate to contact me if you require any further information or assistance.

Sincerely,

[Your Name]

Response: Introduction:
This response will explore a lively dialogue between two individuals, one in a ball gown and the other in sweatpants, as they prepare for an evening gala. The conversation will delve into their anticipation, misgivings, and expectations for the night, highlighting the humor, curiosity, and awkwardness of their interaction.

Body:
As they stood outside the gala venue, Emily, resplendent in her shimmering ball gown, and Ryan, clad in his comfortable sweatpants and hoodie, exchanged a glance that spoke volumes about their contrasting attitudes towards the event. Emily, who had spent hours perfecting her look, complete with intricate embroidery and delicate accessories, couldn't help but feel a sense of excitement and nervousness. Ryan, on the other hand, seemed utterly nonchalant, his casual attire a testament to his laid-back approach to the evening.

"I'm not sure what to expect," Emily said, fidgeting with her gloves. "I've heard the guest list is quite impressive, but I'm a bit worried about sticking out like a sore thumb." Ryan chuckled, his eyes crinkling at the corners. "You're going to shine like a diamond, Emily. I'm the one who's going to stick out – like a sore thumb, or rather, a sweaty mess." Emily laughed, her eyes sparkling with amusement. "Well, at least you're comfortable. I feel like I'm suffocating in this corset."

As they entered the venue, they were immediately immersed in a sea of elegantly dressed guests. Ryan's casual attire drew more than a few curious glances, but he seemed to take it in stride. "I'm just here for the free food and drinks," he joked, snagging a glass of champagne from a passing waiter. Emily playfully rolled her eyes. "You're such a philistine, Ryan. This is a night to remember, not just a buffet."

Despite their differences, the two friends navigated the evening with ease, their conversation flowing effortlessly as they mingled with the other guests. They discussed everything from the latest gossip to their shared love of literature, their mutual respect and admiration for each other's unique perspectives and interests evident in every exchange.

Conclusion:
In conclusion, the dialogue between Emily and Ryan showcases the humor, curiosity, and slight awkwardness of their interaction as they prepare for the evening gala. Their contrasting attire serves as a backdrop for their conversation, highlighting their different approaches to the event and their expectations for the night. Through their exchange, it becomes clear that true friendship can transcend superficial differences, and that a shared sense of humor and mutual respect can make even the most unlikely of pairings a perfect match.

Il est essentiel que chaque partie de votre texte respecte cette règle afin d'assurer une immersion linguistique totale. Response: As I stepped off the plane at Narita International Airport, I was immediately struck by the unique blend of traditional and modern elements that define Japan. The sleek, modern architecture of the airport terminal stood in stark contrast to the ancient customs and practices that I would soon encounter during my journey. My first impressions of the country were shaped by the efficient and courteous service I received from the airport staff, who helped me navigate the complex process of collecting my luggage and exchanging currency.

From the airport, I traveled to Tokyo, a city that is renowned for its vibrant energy and stunning skyline. The bustling streets of Shibuya and Shinjuku were a feast for the senses, with towering skyscrapers, neon lights, and a kaleidoscope of sounds and smells that seemed to assault me from every direction. I spent hours exploring the city's many temples and shrines, including the famous Meiji Shrine, which is dedicated to the deified spirits of Emperor Meiji and his wife, Empress Shoken. The tranquility of these sacred spaces provided a welcome respite from the hustle and bustle of city life, and I was struck by the sense of reverence and respect that the Japanese people have for their spiritual heritage.

One of the highlights of my trip was visiting the ancient city of Kyoto, which is home to countless temples, gardens, and other cultural attractions. The Fushimi Inari Shrine, with its thousands of vermillion torii gates, was a particular highlight, and I spent hours hiking through the beautiful forests and gardens that surround the shrine. I also had the opportunity to visit the Kinkaku-ji Temple, which is famous for its stunning golden pavilion, and the Arashiyama Bamboo Grove, which is a serene and picturesque oasis in the heart of the city.

Of course, no trip to Japan would be complete without sampling the local cuisine, which is renowned for its freshness, variety, and exquisite presentation. I spent hours exploring the Tsukiji Outer Market in Tokyo, where I sampled some of the freshest sushi I have ever tasted, and visited a traditional ramen stall in Fukuoka, where I savored a delicious bowl of noodles in a rich, savory broth. I also had the opportunity to indulge in traditional kaiseki dining, which is a multi-course meal that emphasizes local, seasonal ingredients and exquisite presentation.

Throughout my journey, I was struck by the warmth and hospitality of the Japanese people, who were always eager to share their culture and traditions with me. I participated in a traditional tea ceremony, which was a fascinating insight into the country's rich cultural heritage, and attended a sumo wrestling match, which was an exhilarating and unforgettable experience. I also had the opportunity to interact with locals in a variety of settings, from bustling city streets to quiet rural villages, and I was consistently impressed by their kindness, courtesy, and respect for tradition.

For travelers who are planning a trip to Japan, I would recommend taking advantage of the country's efficient public transportation system, which includes high-speed trains, buses, and subways. The Japan Rail Pass is a great option for travelers who want to explore the country, as it provides unlimited access to the train network for a fixed period of time. I would also recommend visiting some of the lesser-known attractions, such as the beautiful island of Naoshima, which is famous for its modern art museums and sculptures, or the historic city of Kanazawa, which is known for its well-preserved Edo-era architecture and beautiful gardens.

As I reflect on my journey to Japan, I am struck by the unique blend of old and new that defines this fascinating country. From the ancient temples and shrines to the cutting-edge technology and modern architecture, Japan is a country that is deeply rooted in tradition, yet constantly evolving and innovating. My trip was a truly unforgettable experience, and I feel grateful to have had the opportunity to immerse myself in the country's rich culture and traditions. As I look back on my journey, I am reminded of the importance of respecting and appreciating the unique customs and practices of other cultures, and I feel inspired to continue exploring and learning about the world around me.

Response: When creating a resume for a recent high school graduate, it is essential to prioritize the most relevant information to showcase their potential and capabilities to potential employers. The first constraint to consider is that the resume must be well-organized and concise, making it easy for hiring managers to quickly identify the candidate's strengths and qualifications.

This section can include proficiency in software applications, programming languages, or other technical skills, as well as interpersonal skills, such as communication, teamwork, and problem-solving.

To make the candidate more appealing to employers, the resume can also include sections on extracurricular activities, volunteer work, or internships. These experiences can demonstrate the candidate's ability to work in a team, take initiative, and develop valuable skills in a real-world setting. For instance, participating in a school club or organization can showcase leadership skills, while volunteer work can highlight a commitment to social responsibility.

In the absence of direct work experience, it is vital to emphasize any experiences that demonstrate the candidate's potential and eagerness to learn. This can include participation in job shadowing programs, career fairs, or industry conferences, which can provide valuable insights into the field and demonstrate a genuine interest in the profession.

By carefully crafting a resume that highlights relevant academic achievements, extracurricular activities, and skills, a recent high school graduate can increase their chances of standing out in a competitive job market. Employers are often looking for candidates who are highly motivated, enthusiastic, and eager to learn, so it is essential to convey these qualities through a well-structured and effective resume.

In terms of additional experiences, the candidate can consider including any relevant certifications, licenses, or training programs they have completed. This can include certifications in first aid, CPR, or other specialized skills, which can be highly valuable in certain industries. Furthermore, any experience with social media, content creation, or digital marketing can be highly attractive to employers, as these skills are increasingly important in today's digital landscape.

Ultimately, the key to creating a successful resume is to showcase the candidate's unique strengths, skills, and experiences in a clear and concise manner. By prioritizing the most relevant information and tailoring the resume to the specific job or industry, a recent high school graduate can increase their chances of securing an entry-level position and launching a successful career.

- Name: Emily J. Smith

- Strong teamwork and collaboration abilities
- Effective problem-solving and time management skills
