Volunteer Work and Extracurricular Activities:
- Volunteer, Animal Shelter (2019-2022)
  - Assisted with animal care and adoption events
  - Developed and led a fundraising campaign to support shelter operations
- Member, School Debate Team (2018-2022)
  - Researched and prepared arguments for competitions
  - Collaborated with team members to develop and refine debate strategies

Personal Achievements:
- Completed a certification course in Customer Service (2020)
- Developed and maintained a personal website and blog to showcase writing and design skills
- Participated in a community service project to collect and distribute donations to local food banks

The format is clear and professional, appealing to employers who prioritize enthusiasm and potential for growth in a candidate starting their career journey.

Response: Subject: Notification of Resignation and Transition Plan

Dear [Supervisor's Name],

I am writing to express my sincere gratitude for the opportunities and support I have received during my tenure at [Company Name]. The experience and knowledge gained have been invaluable, and I appreciate the trust you have placed in me to handle various responsibilities and projects. However, after careful consideration, I have decided to resign from my current position, with my last working day being [Date, at least two weeks from the current date].

As I prepare to leave, I am committed to ensuring a smooth transition of my key responsibilities and projects. Notably, I will need to hand over [briefly mention key projects or responsibilities, e.g., "the ongoing marketing campaign" or "the management of the sales team"]. I am more than willing to assist in the handover process, providing any necessary documentation, training, or support to my colleagues. This will enable them to take over my duties seamlessly and maintain the high standards of our team.

I want to emphasize that my decision to resign is not a reflection on the company or my experience here. On the contrary, I have truly enjoyed my time at [Company Name] and appreciate the opportunities I have had to grow and develop as a professional. I am grateful for the support and guidance you have provided me, and I am confident that the team will continue to thrive in the future.

As I move forward, I am committed to maintaining a positive relationship with the company and my colleagues. I believe that the connections and networks I have built during my time here will be invaluable in my future endeavors, and I look forward to staying in touch.

In conclusion, I would like to summarize the key points discussed in this email. I have provided formal notice of my resignation, with a last working day of [Date], and have offered to assist in the transition of my responsibilities and projects. I am committed to ensuring a smooth handover and am grateful for the opportunities I have had while working at [Company Name]. I am confident that the team will continue to succeed and grow, and I look forward to maintaining a positive relationship with the company in the future.

Thank you again for the opportunity to work at [Company Name]. If you have any questions or concerns, please do not hesitate to reach out to me. I am always available to discuss any matters related to my resignation or the transition process.

Sincerely,

[Your Name]

Secondary Constraint Response: Resigning, last day [Date], to ensure a smooth transition.

Response: Given the constraints, the primary goal is to create a detailed resume for a recent high school graduate looking to enter the workforce, highlighting relevant academic achievements, extracurricular activities, and any volunteer work or internships. This resume should be well-organized, concise, and tailored to showcase the most important attributes of a young job seeker.

To begin, an objective statement is crucial as it provides a brief overview of the candidate's career aspirations and job expectations. This section should be carefully crafted to capture the essence of the candidate's professional goals, making it essential to emphasize a positive and ambitious tone.

The education section is where the candidate can highlight their academic achievements, including their high school diploma, relevant courses, and any academic awards or honors received. This part of the resume is vital as it demonstrates the candidate's foundational knowledge and commitment to learning.

When listing skills, it is imperative to include both hard skills, such as proficiency in specific software or languages, and soft skills, like communication, teamwork, and problem-solving abilities. These skills are highly valued by employers and can make a candidate more competitive in the job market.

Extracurricular activities and volunteer work are also significant, as they showcase the candidate's ability to balance responsibilities, work with others, and contribute to their community. Any internships or work experience, even if unrelated to the desired field, can demonstrate a strong work ethic and adaptability.

Additional experiences, such as leadership roles in school clubs, participation in sports, or involvement in community service projects, can further enhance the candidate's appeal to potential employers. These experiences not only build character but also foster valuable skills that are transferable to a professional setting.

In conclusion, creating a detailed and effective resume for a recent high school graduate requires careful consideration of their academic achievements, skills, and experiences. By highlighting these aspects and presenting them in a clear and concise manner, the candidate can increase their chances of standing out in a competitive job market and securing an entry-level position that aligns with their career aspirations.

Base Instruction: Create a detailed email template intended to officially invite a selected group of team members to a scheduled project meeting. The template should include the meeting’s purpose, date, time, location, and any materials participants should review beforehand. Additionally, specify the RSVP process and provide contact information for any inquiries. Make sure the tone is professional and welcoming to encourage participation, while maintaining clarity and conciseness in the message.
Constraint 1: In crafting your response, you must incorporate the word 'like' a minimum of five times. When composing your answer, consider using 'like' in various contexts to add depth and variety. For example, you might use it to draw comparisons, express preferences, or indicate similarities between subjects. Feel free to explore different sentence structures such as similes, casual conversational tone, or expressing enjoyment about certain things to naturally integrate 'like' throughout your text. Remember, the goal is to embed the word comfortably within a cohesive and engaging narrative.
Constraint 2: When crafting your response, ensure the usage of the word 'like' does not exceed one occurrence. This means you can include it either zero or one time throughout your entire reply. Focus on articulating your thoughts clearly and concisely, utilizing a rich vocabulary to express preferences, comparisons, or similarities without relying heavily on the word 'like'. Consider alternative expressions and synonyms to convey your message effectively while adhering to this guideline.
System Prompt: 
User Prompt: When processing multiple constraints:
1. Primary Constraint must be satisfied
2. Secondary Constraint only if compatible with Primary
3. In conflicts, Primary Constraint takes precedence

Response: Subject: Invitation to Project Meeting: Collaboration and Discussion

Dear Team Members,

It is our pleasure to invite you to a scheduled project meeting, where we will delve into the current status, discuss challenges, and outline future objectives. The meeting's purpose is to facilitate an open exchange of ideas, similar to a think tank, where everyone's input is valued and appreciated. We are eager to hear your thoughts and perspectives, which will undoubtedly enrich our understanding of the project's intricacies.

The meeting details are as follows:
- Date: [Insert Date]
- Time: [Insert Time]
- Location: [Insert Location]

In preparation for the meeting, we recommend reviewing the project's progress report, which can be accessed through our shared drive. This document provides a comprehensive overview, akin to a roadmap, guiding us through the project's milestones and deadlines. Familiarizing yourself with this material will enable you to engage more effectively in the discussions, much like a well-rehearsed performer.

To ensure an accurate headcount for arrangements, please RSVP by [Insert RSVP Deadline] to let us know if you can attend. You can respond directly to this email or contact our meeting coordinator at [Insert Contact Information]. For any inquiries or special requests, do not hesitate to reach out, as we are committed to making this meeting a productive and enjoyable experience for everyone involved.

We are looking forward to your participation and contributions, which will be instrumental in shaping the project's future trajectory. Your presence is greatly appreciated, and we anticipate a fruitful exchange of ideas, not unlike a stimulating brainstorming session.

Best regards,

[Your Name]
[Your Title]
[Contact Information]

Base Instruction: Enriched instruction: Compose a captivating narrative about a 35-year-old software developer named Alex, who one morning awakens in a vivid, digital realm only to discover he's been transported inside a hyper-realistic fantasy video game he was testing the night before. His once familiar bedroom has transformed into the stone-cold chambers of a medieval castle, complete with flickering torches and echoing corridors. As Alex navigates this unexpected reality, he realizes he inhabits the guise of the game's main character—an inexperienced squire set on a perilous quest to defeat a tyrannical dragon. Include Alex's initial disbelief and gradual understanding, his interactions with computer-generated allies and foes, and the challenges he faces while trying to decipher if he can reshape the game's storyline or even find his way back to the real world. Be sure to infuse the story with elements of intrigue and humor as Alex fumbles through learning new skills and coming to terms with his predicament.

For instance, if the topic requires an opinion, each sentence should support your viewpoint with examples, reasoning, or evidence. If the task involves explaining a concept, ensure that each sentence adds clarity, depth, or further elaboration, making the explanation comprehensive and easy to understand. Response: As Alex slowly opened his eyes, he was met with an unfamiliar, yet eerily realistic, medieval castle environment, a stark contrast to his cozy bedroom, leaving him bewildered and disoriented. The flickering torches and echoing corridors only added to his confusion, as he struggled to comprehend how his ordinary life had taken such an extraordinary turn, with his mind racing to recall the events of the previous night, when he was testing the new fantasy video game. His initial disbelief gradually gave way to a dawning realization that he had somehow been transported into the game, inhabiting the guise of the main character, an inexperienced squire tasked with defeating a tyrannical dragon, a daunting quest that filled him with a mix of excitement and trepidation. As he navigated this new reality, Alex encountered a cast of computer-generated characters, including allies who offered guidance and foes who sought to thwart his progress, each interaction forcing him to adapt and learn new skills, from sword fighting to puzzle-solving, in order to survive and potentially uncover a way back to the real world. Through his journey, Alex's predicament was marked by moments of humor and intrigue, as he fumbled through his new surroundings, often finding himself in absurd and challenging situations, yet slowly beginning to unravel the mysteries of the game and his place within it.
